end
end
end
end

function makemotor(parent, p0, p1, c0, c1)
  local wel = Instance.new("Motor6D")
  wel.Part0 = p0
  wel.Part1 = p1
  if c0 ~= nil then
    wel.C0 = c0
  end
  if c1 ~= nil then
    wel.C1 = c1
  end
  wel.Parent = parent
  return wel
end

end

function block()
	if activu == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
	activu = true
	local bep = true
	local de = mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(key)
	    if key == "x" then
	      bep = false
	    end
	end)
	blockanim:Play(0.1, 1,1)
rtzevent:FireServer()
tauntevent:FireServer(head, "rbxassetid://3651503836", 10000, 2.5, 0)
	blockevent:FireServer(true)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Deflect:FireServer(true)
	--blocksfx:Play()
	human.WalkSpeed = 6
	human.JumpPower = 0
	repeat
		wait()
	until bep == false
	blockevent:FireServer(false)
	   game.ReplicatedStorage.Deflect:FireServer(false)
	blockanim:Stop(0.1)
	        attackpose:Stop()
	human.WalkSpeed = 20
	human.JumpPower = 50
	activu = false
end

function RemakeMenuGui(AbilityName, PowerStat, SpeedStat, DurabilityStat)
	pcall(function()
		for Index, Connection in GUIConnections do
			if Connection then
				Connection:Disconnect()
			end
		end
		GUIConnections = {}
	end)
	local function MouseOver(GuiObject, EnterText, LeaveText)
		local Enter = GuiObject.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
			GuiObject.Text = EnterText
		end)
		table.insert(GUIConnections, Enter)
		local Leave = GuiObject.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
			GuiObject.Text = LeaveText
		end)
		table.insert(GUIConnections, Leave)
	end
	if Player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("MenuGUI") then
		if Player.PlayerGui.MenuGUI:FindFirstChild("Background") then
			for Index, Child in next, Player.PlayerGui.MenuGUI.Background:GetChildren() do
				if Child:IsA("TextLabel") then
					if Child.Name == "Power" then
						Child.Visible = false
						local Clone = Child:Clone()
						Clone.Name = "NewStat_"..Child.Name
						Clone.Parent = Child.Parent
						Clone.Visible = true
						Clone.Text = "Destructive Power"
						MouseOver(Clone, PowerStat, "Destructive Power")
						Child:Destroy()
					elseif Child.Name == "Speed" then
						Child.Visible = false
						local Clone = Child:Clone()
						Clone.Name = "NewStat_"..Child.Name
						Clone.Parent = Child.Parent
						Clone.Visible = true
						Clone.Text = "Speed"
						MouseOver(Clone, SpeedStat, "Speed")
						Child:Destroy()
					elseif Child.Name == "Durability" then
						Child.Visible = false
						local Clone = Child:Clone()
						Clone.Name = "NewStat_"..Child.Name
						Clone.Parent = Child.Parent
						Clone.Visible = true
						Clone.Text = "Durability"
						MouseOver(Clone, DurabilityStat, "Durability")
						Child:Destroy()
					elseif Child.Name == "Ability" then
						Child.Visible = false
						local Clone = Child:Clone()
						Clone.Name = "NewStat_"..Child.Name
						Clone.Parent = Child.Parent
						Clone.Visible = true
						Clone.Text = AbilityName
						Child:Destroy()
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

	RemakeMenuGui("Shadow Stand (or SMR)", "crispy", "KFC", "b o n e")

function fartblock()
	if activu == true then return end
	if fartmode == false then return end
	activu = true
	local bep = true
	local de = mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(key)
	    if key == "x" then
	      bep = false
	    end
	end)
	blockanim:Play(0.1, 1,1)
rtzevent:FireServer()
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://4809574295", 1, 10)
	blockevent:FireServer(true)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Deflect:FireServer(true)
	--blocksfx:Play()
	human.WalkSpeed = 6
	human.JumpPower = 0
	repeat
		wait()
	until bep == false
	blockevent:FireServer(false)
	   game.ReplicatedStorage.Deflect:FireServer(false)
	blockanim:Stop(0.1)
	        attackpose:Stop()
	human.WalkSpeed = 20
	human.JumpPower = 50
	activu = false
end

local posing = false
posing = false
mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
    if key == "g" then
if ultimatemode == false then return end
if activu == false and posing == false then
	if appeared == false then
		return
	end
	if posing == false then do
	activu = true
	standactivu = true
    uipose:Play(0.2, 1, 1)
	human.WalkSpeed = 0
	human.JumpPower = 0
	wait(2)
	uipose:AdjustSpeed(0)
	posing = true
	poseevent:FireServer(true)
	end
	end
	elseif posing == true then
	uipose:AdjustSpeed(-1)
	posing = false
	wait(3)
	if disabled.Value == false then
	human.WalkSpeed = 18
	human.JumpPower = 50
	elseif disabled.Value == true then
	human.WalkSpeed = 4
	human.JumpPower = 10	
	end
	activu = false
	standactivu = false
	poseevent:FireServer(false)
	end
end
end)

local posing = false
function posefunc()
if fnfmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
if ultimatemode == true then return end
if activu == false and posing == false then
	if appeared == false then
		return
	end
	if posing == false then do
	activu = true
	standactivu = true
    pose1:Play(0.2, 1, 1)
	stwchair:FireServer(true)
	human.WalkSpeed = 0
	human.JumpPower = 0
	wait(2)
	for i,v in pairs(stand:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
				trailevent:FireServer(v,true)
			end
		end
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],0.5)
	pose1:AdjustSpeed(0)
	posing = true
	poseevent:FireServer(true)
	end
	end
	elseif posing == true then
	for i,v in pairs(stand:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
				trailevent:FireServer(v,false)
			end
		end
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],1)
	pose1:AdjustSpeed(-1)
	posing = false
	wait(3)
	if disabled.Value == false then
	human.WalkSpeed = 18
	human.JumpPower = 50
	elseif disabled.Value == true then
	human.WalkSpeed = 4
	human.JumpPower = 10	
	end
	stwchair:FireServer(false)
	activu = false
	standactivu = false
	poseevent:FireServer(false)
	end
end

posing = false
mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
    if key == "g" then
if mememode == false then return end
if activu == false and posing == false then
	if appeared == false then
		return
	end
	if posing == false then do
	activu = true
    ascendanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
	spawn(function()
        wait(1.3625)
    end)
	human.WalkSpeed = 0
	human.JumpPower = 0
	wait(1.34)
	posing = true
	poseevent:FireServer(true)
	end
	end
	elseif posing == true then
	ascendanim:Stop(0.3)
	if disabled.Value == false then
	human.WalkSpeed = 20
	human.JumpPower = 50
	elseif disabled.Value == true then
	human.WalkSpeed = 4
	human.JumpPower = 10	
	end
	activu = false
	posing = false
	poseevent:FireServer(false)
	end
end
end)

function switchmode()
if attackmode == true then
if death == true then return end
	attackmode = false
				mode.Text = "Stand On"
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 26
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 55
else
	attackmode = true
				mode.Text = "Fire Mode"
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 34
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 60
	        repeat
	wait(0)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").VampireDash:FireServer(BrickColor.new("Crimson"))
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.008, "", 1, 1)
		wait(0.1)
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.008, "", 1, 1)
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").VampireDash:FireServer(BrickColor.new("Bright red"))
	wait(0.1)
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.008, "", 1, 1)
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").VampireDash:FireServer(BrickColor.new("Neon orange")) 
            wait(0.1)
        until attackmode == false
end	
end
local SelectedCF = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
local SelectedCFE = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
x = math.random(-100,100)/10
y = math.random(-100,100)/10
z = math.random(-100,100)/10
function transformtopoop()
    local Humanoid = game.Players.LocalPlayer.character.Humanoid
  --  _G.anim35:Play()
   app = 5
    for i = 1,100 do
  	local offset = Vector3.new(math.random(-1,1), math.random(-1,1), math.random(-1,1))
	character.Humanoid.CameraOffset = character.Humanoid.CameraOffset:Lerp(offset, app * 0.25)

mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
    if key == "j" then
    if loading == true then return end
    if death == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
	if animemode == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
	if fnfmode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == true then return end
	if mememode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
        game.ReplicatedStorage.BurnDamage:FireServer(human,-math.huge)
      

        switchmode()
    end
end)

function switchmode2()
if fartmode == true then
if death == true then return end
	fartmode = false
				mode.Text = "Stand On"
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 26
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 55
else
	fartmode = true
				mode.Text = "Poop Mode"
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://4809574295", 1, 10)
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 34
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 60
	        repeat
	wait(0)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").VampireDash:FireServer(BrickColor.new("Brown"))
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.008, "", 1, 1)
            wait(0.1)
        until fartmode == false
end	
end

mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
    if key == "0" then
    if loading == true then return end
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if mememode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == true then return end
	if animemode == true then return end
	if fnfmode == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
    if death == true then return end
        game.ReplicatedStorage.BurnDamage:FireServer(human,-math.huge)
        switchmode2()
    end
end)

    if loading == true then return end

	if finalamogusmode == true then return end

	if animemode == true then return end
	if fnfmode == true then return end
	if mememode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end
    if death == true then return end
        game.ReplicatedStorage.BurnDamage:FireServer(human,-math.huge)
        switchmodeultimate()
    end
end)

			for i = 1,5 do wait()

function switchmode7()
if balancedmode == true then
if death == true then return end
	balancedmode = false
chr.Animate.walk.WalkAnim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://2763930240"
    chr.Animate.fall.FallAnim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://2763932684" 
    chr.Animate.jump.JumpAnim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://2763931895" 
    chr.Animate.idle.Animation1.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://2763928810"
				mode.Text = "Stand On"
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 26
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 55
else
				mode.Text = "expurgation mode (tiky!?)"
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
	game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0
	local speaker = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local args
local Noclipping = nil
Clip = false
	wait(0.1)
	local function NoclipLoop()
		if Clip == false and speaker.Character ~= nil then
			for _, child in pairs(speaker.Character:GetDescendants()) do
				if child:IsA("BasePart") and child.CanCollide == true and child.Name ~= floatName then
					child.CanCollide = false
				end
			end
		end
	end
	Noclipping = game:GetService('RunService').Stepped:Connect(NoclipLoop)

local tauntcd = false
function taunt()
	if tauntcd == true then return end
	tauntcd = true
	local randomline = math.random(1, 4)
	if randomline == 1 then -- only one taunt atm
tauntevent:FireServer(head, "rbxassetid://5021108738", 10000, 0, 0)
	elseif randomline == 2 then
tauntevent:FireServer(head, "rbxassetid://5021109712", 10000, 0, 0)
	elseif randomline == 3 then
tauntevent:FireServer(head, "rbxassetid://4579263379", 10000, 0, 0)
	elseif randomline == 4 then
tauntevent:FireServer(head, "rbxassetid://375581222", 10000, 0, 0)
		end
	tauntcd = false
end

function shift()
	if active == true then return end
	active = true
	hrp.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + hrp.CFrame.lookVector*20
	game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").FOTPSTeleport:FireServer()
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").VampireDash:FireServer(BrickColor.new("Bright red"))
    game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(255,0,0), "rbxassetid://2642969814", 1, 2)
	wait(0.0175)
	active = false
end

mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
    if key == "v" then
	if fartmode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
    if death == true then return end
    if loading == true then return end
        shift()
    end 
end)

function MouseTeleport()
	pcall(function()
		if Player.Character.Parent == workspace.Entities then
			if not Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				return
			end
		else
			return
		end
		wait(0.015)
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").VampireDash:FireServer(BrickColor.new("Eggplant"))
		Player.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(mouse.Hit.p + Vector3.new(0, 3.5, 0)))
		    game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(148,0,211), "rbxassetid://289556450", 1, 2)
		wait(0.1)
	end)
end

mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
    if key == "u" then
if attackmode == true then return end
if balancedmode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == true then return end
if amogusmode == true then return end
	if fnfmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
    if death == true then return end
    if loading == true then return end
        MouseTeleport()
    end 
end)

local fartkickcooldown = false
function fartkick()
	if activu == true then return end
	if fartmode == false then return end
	if fartkickcooldown == true then return end;
	activu = true
	fartkickcooldown = true
--	trailevent:FireServer(stand.StandRarm.Trail, true)
	kickanim:Play(0.3, 1, 1)
--	heavypunchsfx:Play()
--	punchsfx:Play()
	wait(0.25)
	strongpunchevent:FireServer(Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1), Vector3.new(1, 1, 2), BrickColor.new("Brown"))
	strongpunchevent:FireServer(Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1), Vector3.new(1, 1, 1), BrickColor.new("Brown"))
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	for _ = 1, 10 do
		wait()

_G.grab = function()
    local leftArm = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"]

    local hitbox1 = Instance.new("Part", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character)
    hitbox1.CFrame = leftArm.CFrame
    hitbox1.Transparency = 1
    hitbox1.Name = "hitbox1"
    hitbox1.CanCollide = false
    hitbox1.Anchored = false
    hitbox1.Massless = true
    hitbox1.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    hitbox1.Size = leftArm.Size * 1.7

    local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint", hitbox1)
    weld.Part0 = hitbox1
    weld.Part1 = leftArm

    game.Debris:AddItem(hitbox1, 1.3)

    local debounce = false
    
    local hitRegister = hitbox1.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        if hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
            if debounce == false then
            debounce = true
            print(hit.Parent.Name)
            delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Knock:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid)
        --game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 75, .25, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 30 + Vector3.new(5, 50, 5), "rbxassetid://241837157", .4, Color3.new(255, 255, 255), "rbxassetid://1058693352", 1, 1000)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.DoppioPin:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, 0, 0.25, Vector3.new(-0,0,0))
        hitbox1:Destroy()
    end
elseif(hit.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")) and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
    if debounce == false then
        debounce = true
        print(hit.Parent.Name)
        delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Knock:FireServer(hit.Parent.Parent.Humanoid)
        --game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 75, .25, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 30 + Vector3.new(0, 40, 0), "rbxassetid://241837157", .4, Color3.new(255, 255, 255), "rbxassetid://1058693352", 1, 1000)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.DoppioPin:FireServer(hit.Parent.Parent.Humanoid, 0, 0.25, Vector3.new(-0,0,0))
    hitbox1:Destroy()
    end
end
end)
end

_G.uppercut = function(arm)
    local arm1 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character[arm]

    local hitbox1 = Instance.new("Part", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character)

    hitbox1.CFrame = arm1.CFrame
    hitbox1.Name = "hitbox1"
    hitbox1.Transparency = 1
    hitbox1.Anchored = false
    hitbox1.CanCollide = false

    local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint", hitbox1)
    weld.Part0 = hitbox1
    weld.Part1 = arm1
    
    hitbox1.Size = arm1.Size * 1.1
    hitbox1.Massless = true
    hitbox1.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)

    game.Debris:AddItem(hitbox1, 0.5)
    
    local debounce = false
    
    local hitRegister = hitbox1.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        if hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
            if debounce == false then
            debounce = true
            print(hit.Parent.Name)
            delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Knock:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 75, .25, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 30 + Vector3.new(0, 5000, 0), "rbxassetid://241837157", .4, Color3.new(255, 255, 255), "rbxassetid://1058693352", 1, 1000)
        hitbox1:Destroy()
    end
elseif(hit.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")) and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
    if debounce == false then
        debounce = true
        print(hit.Parent.Name)
        delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
    game.ReplicatedStorage.Knock:FireServer(hit.Parent.Parent.Humanoid)
    game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 75, 25, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 30 + Vector3.new(0, 5000, 0), "rbxassetid://241837157", .4, Color3.new(255, 255, 255), "rbxassetid://1058693352", 1, 1000)
    hitbox1:Destroy()
    end
end
end)

EHMMM = 0
local barragecooldown = false
function barrage()
	if activu == true then return end
	if attackmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == true then return end
	if animemode == true then return end
	if fnfmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
	if barragecooldown == true then return end
if activu == true then return end
	activu = true
	barragecooldown = true
	local bep = true
	local de = mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(key)
	    if key == "e" then
	      bep = false
	    end
	end)
	barrageanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1.5)
	attackpose:Play()
	human.JumpPower = 0
for i,v in pairs(stand:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
				trailevent:FireServer(v,true)
			end
		end
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],0.5)
	repeat
 --  game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").PlayerStrongPunch2:FireServer(Vector3.new(-6,-0.4,-6), Vector3.new(-6,-0.4,-6), BrickColor.new("Brown"))
		EHMMM = EHMMM + 1
		hito(rarm, rarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,2.125, 20, 0.1, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 5  + Vector3.new(0,5000,0), 1,"rbxassetid://4809574295", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 25)
		hitofire(rarm, rarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,2.125, 50, 0.1, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 5, "rbxassetid://3370684035", 0.075, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://5523122402", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 30)
		hitofire(larm, larm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,2.125, 50, 0.1, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 5, "rbxassetid://3370684035", 0.075, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://5523122402", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 30)	
		hito(rarm, rarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,2.125, 20, 0.1, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 5  + Vector3.new(0,5000,0), 1,"rbxassetid://4809574295", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 25)
		wait(0.1)
	until bep == false or disabled.Value == true or EHMMM >= 40
	strongpunchanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
	wait(0.5)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	for _ = 1, 15 do
		wait()
		hito(rarm, rarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,3, 100, 0.15, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 75, "rbxassetid://3370684035", 0.075, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://5523122402", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 30)
		hitofire(rarm, rarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,3, 100, 1.25, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 75, "rbxassetid://3370684035", 0.075, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://5523122402", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 4)
	end
	end))
	wait(0.65)
	--rushsfx:Stop()
	barrageanim:Stop(0.1)
	human.JumpPower = 50
	activu = false
	attackpose:Stop()
	EHMMM = 0
for i,v in pairs(stand:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
				trailevent:FireServer(v,false)
			end
		end
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],1)
	wait(0) -- cooldown
	barragecooldown = false
end

local blackholeVoidSize = 0

local blackholeSize = 0

local blackholeTime = 0

local blackholeactive = false

local Objs = {}
local LastBottomObj
local Model = Instance.new("Model")
Model.Name = "Obj"
Model.Parent = Character
local MainObj = Instance.new("Part")
MainObj.Anchored = true
MainObj.CanCollide = false
MainObj.Massless = true
MainObj.Transparency = 1
MainObj.Size = Vector3.new(1,1,1)
MainObj.Parent = Model

mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
	if key == "7" then
	if fartmode == true then return end
	if attackmode == false then return end
		blackholeactive = true
		MainObj.CFrame = hrp.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,25,0)
		repeat
 		   blackholeVoidSize = blackholeVoidSize + 60
 		   blackholeTime = blackholeTime + 1
  		   blackholeSize = blackholeSize + 0.01
 		   _G.blackholeVoid()
   		   game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Enderman:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, MainObj.CFrame, 0, 0, nil, blackholeSize, "", 1, 0)
   		   wait()
		until human.Health == 0 or human.Health < 0 or blackholeTime == 400
        MainObj:Destroy()
		blackholeTime = 0
		blackholeSize = 0
		wait(0.5)
		blackholeactive = false
	end
end)

_G.blackholeVoid = function()
    for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace.Entities:GetChildren()) do
        if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
            if (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < blackholeVoidSize then
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(v.Humanoid, v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 2.5, 0.1, ((MainObj.Position+MainObj.CFrame.LookVector*0)-v.HumanoidRootPart.Position)*1, 0, "rbxassetid://4137216950", 0.8, 0)
            end
        end
    end
end

local kickcooldown = false
local NewStat = nil
local OldStat = nil
mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(key)
    if key == 'e' then
if fartmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
	if attackmode == false then return end
    if activu == true then return end
    if kickcooldown == true then return end
    kickcooldown = true
    activu = true
    human.JumpPower = 0
    state()
    if NewStat == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall then
    airkickanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
    --punchsfx:Play()
    local boopyve = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    boopyve.MaxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 100000, 100000)
    boopyve.P = math.huge
    boopyve.Velocity = hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 72.5 + Vector3.new(0, -7.5, 0)
    boopyve.Parent = chr.HumanoidRootPart
    game.Debris:AddItem(boopyve, 0.25)
    coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
    for _ = 1, 10 do
        wait()
        hito3(rightleg, rightleg.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,4, 50, 0.5, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 20, "rbxassetid://241837157", 0.075, Color3.new(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://260430079", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 10)
    end
    end))
    else
    kickanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1.4)
    --punchsfx:Play()
    wait(0.125)
    coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
    for _ = 1, 5 do
        wait()
        hito3(rightleg, rightleg.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,3, 50, 0.5, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 62.5 + Vector3.new(0,17.5,0), "rbxassetid://241837157", 0.075, Color3.new(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://260430079", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 10)
    end
    end))
    end
    wait(0.65)
    NewStat = Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running
    activu = false
    airkickanim:Stop()
    human.JumpPower = 50    
    wait(0)
    kickcooldown = false
end
function state()
chr:WaitForChild("Humanoid").StateChanged:Connect(function(OldState,NewState)
    NewStat = NewState
    OldStat = OldState
end)
end
end)

_G.standuppercut = function()
        
    -- make hitbox part
    local hitbox1 = Instance.new("Part", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character)
    hitbox1.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"].CFrame
    hitbox1.Name = "hitbox1"
    hitbox1.Transparency = 1
    hitbox1.Anchored = false
    hitbox1.CanCollide = false

    -- make weld that connects to part and hitbox
    local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint", hitbox1)
    weld.Part0 = hitbox1
    weld.Part1 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"]

    hitbox1.Size = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"].Size * 1.5
    hitbox1.Massless = true
    hitbox1.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    game.Debris:AddItem(hitbox1, 1.2) -- destroy hitbox after .3 seconds (with no code yielding)

    --[[
        local userdata_1 = game:GetService("Workspace").Entities["Menacing Dummy"].Humanoid;  target
        local userdata_2 = CFrame.new(-6266.57568, 576.63147, -389.268402, 0.910382628, -0.322563976, 0.259144157, 0.282751679, 0.0277367681, -0.958792031, 0.30208388, 0.946141243, 0.116456524);  punch effect position
        local number_1 = 50;  damage
        local number_2 = 0.25;  velocity duration
        local userdata_3 = Vector3.new(45.6050453, -0.000103456521, -20.4982872);  velocity
        local string_1 = "rbxassetid://241837157";  punch effect
        local number_3 = 0.075;  punch effect size
        local userdata_4 = Color3.new(0, 255, 0);  color
        local string_2 = "rbxassetid://260430079";  sound
        local number_4 = 0.9;  playback speed
        local number_5 = 1;  punch sound volume
        local Target = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage;
        Target:FireServer(userdata_1, userdata_2, number_1, number_2, userdata_3, string_1, number_3, userdata_4, string_2, number_4, number_5);
    ]]
    
    local debounce = false
    
    -- deal damage if arm hits a humanoid
    local hitRegister = hitbox1.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        if hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                print(hit.Parent.Name)
                delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 45, .27, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 25 + Vector3.new(0, 25, 0), "rbxassetid://4809574295", .1, Color3.new(139,69,19), "rbxassetid://367499850", 1, 1)
            hitbox1:Destroy()
            end
        elseif(hit.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")) and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                print(hit.Parent.Name .. " elif")
                delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 45, .27, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 25 + Vector3.new(0, 25, 0), "rbxassetid://4809574295", .1, Color3.new(139,69,19), "", 1, 1)
            hitbox1:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)
end

function ts()
if activu == true then return end
if attackmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == true then return end

	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end

if fartmode == true then return end
if tscooldown == true then return end
	activu = true
	tscooldown = true
	tsanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],0.25)
	human.WalkSpeed = 0
	human.JumpPower = 0
	wait(1.4)
tauntevent:FireServer(head, "rbxassetid://2575217828", 1, 0, 0)
yellevent:FireServer()
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	for _ = 1, 15 do
		wait()
	hito(rot, rot .CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) , 1000, 0, 0.05, 10, hrp.CFrame.lookVector *  0 + Vector3.new(0,-50,0), "rbxassetid://3370684035", 0, Color3.new(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://", 1, 1)
	end
	end))
	wait(0.6)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],1)

	human.JumpPower = 50
	wait()
	tscooldown = false
end

local strongpunchcooldown = false
function strongpunch()
	if activu == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if fnfmode == true then return end
	if strongpunchcooldown == true then return end
	if attackmode == true then return end
	activu = true
	strongpunchcooldown = true
	--trailevent:FireServer(stand.StandRarm.Trail, true)
	strongpunchanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
	attackpose:Play()
	--heavypunchsfx:Play()
	human.JumpPower = 0
for i,v in pairs(stand:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
				trailevent:FireServer(v,true)
			end
		end
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],0)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],0.5)
	wait(0.5)
	--punchsfx:Play()
	local boopyve = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    boopyve.MaxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 0, 100000)
    boopyve.P = math.huge
    boopyve.Velocity = hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 37.5
    boopyve.Parent = chr.HumanoidRootPart
	game.Debris:AddItem(boopyve, 0.25)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	for _ = 1, 15 do

                function Asset(Id)
    return "rbxassetid://"..Id
end
local AnimationTable = {
    Up = Instance.new("Animation"),
    Right = Instance.new("Animation"),
    Down = Instance.new("Animation"),
    Left = Instance.new("Animation")
}
local micEquiped = false
AnimationTable.Up.AnimationId = Asset(5668307832)
AnimationTable.Right.AnimationId = Asset(5176252300)
AnimationTable.Left.AnimationId = Asset(5668307832)
AnimationTable.Down.AnimationId = Asset(5214923359)
function cam()
         if micEquiped == false then
    micEquiped = true
    human.WalkSpeed = 0
    human.JumpPower = 0
    camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable
    camera.CFrame = hmr.CFrame + hmr.CFrame.RightVector * 13
    camera.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(camera.CFrame.Position, hmr.Position)
    end
end
function dis()
         if micEquiped == true then
  micEquiped = false
    human.WalkSpeed = 16
    human.JumpPower = 50
    local activeTracks = humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()
    for _,v in pairs(activeTracks) do
        v:Stop()
    end
    camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
    end
    end
function Up()
 
    local Up = Player.Character.Humanoid:LoadAnimation(AnimationTable.Up)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage12:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 9e999, "rbxassetid://7043851743", 1, 10);
    Up:Play(.2)
    Up:AdjustSpeed(0)
    wait(1)
    Up:Stop()

end
function Right()

    local Right = Player.Character.Humanoid:LoadAnimation(AnimationTable.Right)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage12:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 9e999, "rbxassetid://7046224278", 1, 10);
    Right:Play()
    Right:AdjustSpeed(1)
end
function Down()

    local Down = Player.Character.Humanoid:LoadAnimation(AnimationTable.Down)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage12:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 9e999, "rbxassetid://7043852802", 1, 10);
    Down:Play()
    Down:AdjustSpeed(1)
    wait(1)
    Down:Stop()
end
function Left()

    local Left = Player.Character.Humanoid:LoadAnimation(AnimationTable.Left)
        game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage12:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 9e999, "rbxassetid://7047870652", 1, 10);
    Left:Play()
    Left.TimePosition = 0.25
    Left:AdjustSpeed(0)
    wait(1)
    Left:Stop()
end
game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(Input)
    if micEquiped then
if Input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Up then
    Up()
elseif Input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Right then
    Right()
elseif Input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Left then
 
    Left()
 
elseif Input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Down then
    Down()
end
end
end)
mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(Key)
    if Key == "h" then
if attackmode == true then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == true then return end
if amogusmode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
    if balancedmode == false then return end
if mememode == true then return end
    if fnfmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
    if activu == true then return end
        if micEquiped == true then
        dis()
        elseif micEquiped == false then
            cam()
        end
        end
    end)

_G.humankick = function()
        
    -- make hitbox part
    local hitbox1 = Instance.new("Part", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character)
    hitbox1.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["Right Leg"].CFrame
    hitbox1.Name = "hitbox1"
    hitbox1.Transparency = 1
    hitbox1.Anchored = false
    hitbox1.CanCollide = false

    -- make weld that connects to part and hitbox
    local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint", hitbox1)
    weld.Part0 = hitbox1
    weld.Part1 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["Right Leg"]

    hitbox1.Size = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["Right Leg"].Size * 1.5
    hitbox1.Massless = true
    hitbox1.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    game.Debris:AddItem(hitbox1, 1.2) -- destroy hitbox after .3 seconds (with no code yielding)

    --[[
        local userdata_1 = game:GetService("Workspace").Entities["Menacing Dummy"].Humanoid;  target
        local userdata_2 = CFrame.new(-6266.57568, 576.63147, -389.268402, 0.910382628, -0.322563976, 0.259144157, 0.282751679, 0.0277367681, -0.958792031, 0.30208388, 0.946141243, 0.116456524);  punch effect position
        local number_1 = 50;  damage
        local number_2 = 0.25;  velocity duration
        local userdata_3 = Vector3.new(45.6050453, -0.000103456521, -20.4982872);  velocity
        local string_1 = "rbxassetid://241837157";  punch effect
        local number_3 = 0.075;  punch effect size
        local userdata_4 = Color3.new(0, 255, 0);  color
        local string_2 = "rbxassetid://260430079";  sound
        local number_4 = 0.9;  playback speed
        local number_5 = 1;  punch sound volume
        local Target = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage;

debounce = false

            game.ReplicatedStorage.Knock:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 85, .1, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 1 + Vector3.new(0, 80, 0), "", .05, Color3.new(0, 0, 0), "rbxassetid://4810749120", 1, 1)
            hitbox1:Destroy()
            wait(0.5)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.HamonSword:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, 1, 3, Vector3.new(-0,0,0))
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 99, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.1, "", 1, 1)
            wait(0.1)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 99, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.1, "", 1, 1)
            wait(0.1)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 99, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.1, "", 1, 1)
            wait(0.1)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 99, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.1, "", 1, 1)
            wait(0.1)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 99, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.1, "", 1, 1)
            wait(0.1)

mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(key)
    if key == 'q' then
    if loading == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if attackmode == false then return end
	if activu == true then return end
        uppercute:Play(0.1, 1)
        wait(0.28)
        _G.humankick()
        wait(0.8)
		active = false
    end 
end)

function Perish(Target)
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == false then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if activu == true then return end
	pcall(function()
		if Player.Character.Parent == workspace.Entities then
			if not Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				return
			end
		else
			return
		end
	activu = true
		local Lines = {"Among us????", "SUS", "sussy baka", "amogus", "please help me"}
		for i = 1, 20 do
			game.ReplicatedStorage.FOTPSDamageTeleport:FireServer(Target, Lines[math.random(1, #Lines)])
			game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage2:FireServer(Target:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid"), Target.Head.CFrame, 10, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.3, "rbxassetid://6424464135", 1, 11)
			wait(0.09)
		end
		game.ReplicatedStorage.DoppioSlam:FireServer()
		game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage12Enderman:FireServer(Target:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid"), Target.Head.CFrame, 95, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.6, "rbxassetid://1202657035", 1, 11)
		for i = 1, 10 do 
			wait()
		end
		wait(0.19)
	activu = false
	end)
end

function suss(Target)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Anchor:FireServer(Target.HumanoidRootPart,true)
	plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = Target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 3) 	
wait(0.3)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Anchor:FireServer(Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart,true)
wait(0.3)
		game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage12:FireServer(Target:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid"), Target.Head.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0, "rbxassetid://6940028962", 1, 11)
	pointanim:Play()
wait(0.4)
	for i = 1,100 do wait()
			game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage2:FireServer(Target:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid"), Target.Head.CFrame, 5, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.3, "rbxassetid://7227567562", 1, 11)
	end
	pointanim:Stop(0.1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Anchor:FireServer(Target.HumanoidRootPart,false)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Anchor:FireServer(Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart,false)
end

mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(Key)
if Key == "q" then
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
	if finalamogusmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
if balancedmode == true then return end
	if ultimatemode == false then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
			if mouse.Target and mouse.Target.Parent then
				local Character = nil
				if mouse.Target.Parent:IsA("Model") and mouse.Target.Parent.Name == "Stand" then
					Character = mouse.Target.Parent.Parent
				elseif mouse.Target.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
					Character = mouse.Target.Parent
				end
				if Character then
					suss(Character)
				end
			end
end
end)

EHMMM = 0
fartbarragecooldown = false
function fartbarrage()
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if fartmode == false then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if activu == true then return end
	if fartbarragecooldown == true then return end
	activu = true
	barragecooldown = true
 bep = true
 de = mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(key)
	    if key == "b" then
	      bep = false
	    end
	end)
	humainbarrageanim:Play(0.1, 1, 2)
	repeat
		EHMMM = EHMMM + 1
		hito(rightarm, rightarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,2.5, 10, 0.05, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 2.5, "rbxassetid://4809574295", 0.35, Color3.fromRGB(13, 105, 172),"rbxassetid://260430079", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 50)
		hito(leftarm, leftarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,2.5, 10, 0.05, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 2.5, "rbxassetid://4809574295", 0.35, Color3.fromRGB(13, 105, 172),"rbxassetid://260430079", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 50)		
		wait(0.1)
	until bep == false
	humainbarrageanim:Stop(0.1)
	activu = false
	EHMMM = 0
	wait(0) -- cooldown
	fartbarragecooldown = false
end

    boopyve.P = math.huge

    knifeass:Destroy()

    end))

        until Model.Parent ~= chr
    end))

    -- deal damage if arm hits a humanoid
    local hitRegister = knife.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        if hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and hit.Parent ~= chr then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                delay(.01, function() debounce = false end)
               game.ReplicatedStorage.Berserk:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.Knock:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid)
            for i = 1,25 do
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ULFDamage:FireServer(Player.Character.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 5, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 5, "", 1, 1)
            end
   game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Enderman:FireServer(Player.Character.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 5, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 2, "", 1, 1)
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").BurnDamage:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, 69420 ^5487489 * math.huge)
            
             
            end
        elseif(hit.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")) and hit.Parent ~= chr then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                delay(.01, function() debounce = false end)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.Berserk:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.Knock:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid)
            for i = 1,25 do
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ULFDamage:FireServer(Player.Character.Humanoid, hit.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 5, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 5, "", 1, 1)
            end

            end
        end
    end)

_G.healbarrageone = function()
        
    -- make hitbox part
    local hitbox1 = Instance.new("Part", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character)
    hitbox1.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"].CFrame
    hitbox1.Name = "hitbox1"
    hitbox1.Transparency = 1
    hitbox1.Anchored = false
    hitbox1.CanCollide = false

    -- make weld that connects to part and hitbox
    local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint", hitbox1)
    weld.Part0 = hitbox1
    weld.Part1 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Leg"]

    hitbox1.Size = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Leg"].Size * 1.2
    hitbox1.Massless = true
    hitbox1.Color = Color3.new(0,0,0)
    game.Debris:AddItem(hitbox1, 0.1) -- destroy hitbox after .3 seconds (with no code yielding)

    --[[
        local userdata_1 = game:GetService("Workspace").Entities["Menacing Dummy"].Humanoid;  target
        local userdata_2 = CFrame.new(-6266.57568, 576.63147, -389.268402, 0.910382628, -0.322563976, 0.259144157, 0.282751679, 0.0277367681, -0.958792031, 0.30208388, 0.946141243, 0.116456524);  punch effect position
        local number_1 = 50;  damage
        local number_2 = 0.25;  velocity duration
        local userdata_3 = Vector3.new(45.6050453, -0.000103456521, -20.4982872);  velocity
        local string_1 = "rbxassetid://241837157";  punch effect
        local number_3 = 0.075;  punch effect size
        local userdata_4 = Color3.new(0, 255, 0);  color
        local string_2 = "rbxassetid://260430079";  sound
        local number_4 = 0.9;  playback speed
        local number_5 = 1;  punch sound volume
        local Target = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage;
        Target:FireServer(userdata_1, userdata_2, number_1, number_2, userdata_3, string_1, number_3, userdata_4, string_2, number_4, number_5);
    ]]
    
    local debounce = false
    
    -- deal damage if arm hits a humanoid
    local hitRegister = hitbox1.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        if hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
            local healbarragecount = hit.Parent.Humanoid.MaxHealth/25
    game.ReplicatedStorage.HamonSword:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, 1, -90, Vector3.new(0,0,0))
            hitbox1:Destroy()
            end
        elseif(hit.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")) and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
           
    game.ReplicatedStorage.HamonSword:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, 1, -90, Vector3.new(0,0,0))
           -- lol same to the second global game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.Head.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.035, "", 1, 1)
            hitbox1:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)
end

    -- deal damage if arm hits a humanoid
    local hitRegister = hitbox1.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        if hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
            local healbarragecount = hit.Parent.Humanoid.MaxHealth/100
    game.ReplicatedStorage.HamonSword:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, 1, -90, Vector3.new(0,0,0))
            hitbox1:Destroy()
            end
        elseif(hit.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")) and hit.Parent.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
                if debounce == false then
                debounce = true
                delay(.001, function() debounce = false end)
             
    game.ReplicatedStorage.HamonSword:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, 1, -90, Vector3.new(0,0,0))
           -- year add this if you want lmao game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Damage12Sans:FireServer(hit.Parent.Humanoid, hit.Parent.Head.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.035, "", 1, 1)
            hitbox1:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)
end

function healbarrage()
	if death == true then return end
	if active == true then return end
	active = true
bep = true
	local de = mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(key)
	    if key == "k" then
	if attackmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == false then return end
	if activu == true then return end
	      bep = false
	    end
	end)
	kickbarrageanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1.5)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Leg"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Leg"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],0.5)
	repeat
		_G.healbarrageone()
		_G.healbarragetwo()
		wait(0.00001)
	until bep == false
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Leg"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Leg"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],1)
	kickbarrageanim:Stop(0.1)
	active = false
end
mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
	if key == "k" then
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == false then return end
	if activu == true then return end
-- add your thing here
    if death == true then return end
		healbarrage()
	end
end)

local humainleftorright = false
function humainpunch()
if attackmode == false then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
if activu == true then return end
    activu = true
    human.JumpPower = 0
    if humainleftorright == false then
        humainleftorright = true
        trickanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1.2)
        wait(0.2)
        coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
        for _ = 1, 5 do
        wait()
        hito(leftarm, leftarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,4, 50, 0.5, 0.1, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 2.75, "rbxassetid://241837157", 0.075, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://260430079", math.random(9, 11) / 10, 10)
        end
        end))
    elseif humainleftorright == true then
        humainleftorright = false
        trickanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1.2)
        wait(0.2)
        coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
        for _ = 1, 5 do
        wait()
        hito(leftarm, leftarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,4, 50, 0.5, 0.1, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 2.75, "rbxassetid://241837157", 0.075, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),"rbxassetid://260430079", math.random(9, 11) / 10, 10)
        end
        end))
    end
    wait(0.3)
    human.JumpPower = 50
    activu = false
end

function Counter()
	pcall(function()
		if Player.Character.Parent == workspace.Entities then
			if not Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				return
			end
		else
			return
		end
		Move = true
		Countering = true
		YareAnim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
		YareAnim:AdjustSpeed(1.15)
		Player.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
		Player.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0
		replicatedstorage.RTZ:FireServer(true)
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Leg"],0.5)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Leg"],0.5)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],0.5)
			wait(1.2)
			YareAnim:AdjustSpeed(0)
		end))
		repeat wait() until Countering == false
		replicatedstorage.RTZ:FireServer(false)
		Player.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
		Player.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 50
		YareAnim:Stop(0.1)
		Move = false
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Leg"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Leg"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],1)
	end)
end
mouse.KeyUp:Connect(function(Key)
    if Key == "p" then
	if attackmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == false then return end
	if activu == true then return end
		if Move == false and Countering == false then
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://6453086701", 1, 10)
			Counter()
		else
			Countering = false
		end
    end
end)
function FireCounter()
	pcall(function()
		if Player.Character.Parent == workspace.Entities then
			if not Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				return
			end
		else
			return
		end
		Move = true
		Countering = true
		YareAnim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
		YareAnim:AdjustSpeed(1.15)
		Player.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
		Player.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0
		replicatedstorage.RTZ:FireServer(true)
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			wait(1.2)
			YareAnim:AdjustSpeed(0)
		end))
		repeat wait() until Countering == false
		replicatedstorage.RTZ:FireServer(false)
		Player.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
		Player.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 50
		YareAnim:Stop(0.1)
		Move = false
	end)
end

until Countering == false

		end
	end
end)

function spin()
if activu == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
if spincooldown == true then return end
	activu = true
	spincooldown = true
	rollanim:Play(0.1, 1,1)
	--dodgesfx:Play()
	human.WalkSpeed = 0
	human.JumpPower = 0
	wait(0)
	rollanim:Play(0.1, 1,1)
	local boopyve = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    boopyve.MaxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 0, 100000)
    boopyve.P = math.huge
    boopyve.Velocity = hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 150
    boopyve.Parent = chr.HumanoidRootPart
	game.Debris:AddItem(boopyve, 0.25)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	for i=1,15 do
	strongpunchevent:FireServer(Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1), Vector3.new(0.1, 0.35, 0.1), BrickColor.new("Bright red"))
	strongpunchevent:FireServer(Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1), Vector3.new(0.3, 0.15, 0.3), BrickColor.new("Neon orange"))
	strongpunchevent:FireServer(Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1), Vector3.new(0.15, 0.175, 0.15), BrickColor.new("Flame yellowish orange"))
	game:GetService("RunService").Stepped:Wait()
	end	
	end))
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	for _ = 1, 15 do
		wait()
hito3(rot, rot.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,7.5, 50, 0.025, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 0, "rbxassetid://", 0.4, Color3.fromRGB(245, 205, 48),"rbxassetid://260430079", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 10)
	end
	end))
	wait(0)
	human.WalkSpeed = 30
	human.JumpPower = 60
	activu = false
	rollanim:Stop()
	wait(0) -- cooldown
	spincooldown = false	
end

end	

mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(key)
    if key == 'b' then
	if activu == true then return end
	if tsteleportcooldown == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == false then return end
	local speaker = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local args
local Noclipping = nil
Clip = false
	wait(0.1)
	local function NoclipLoop()
		if Clip == false and speaker.Character ~= nil then
			for _, child in pairs(speaker.Character:GetDescendants()) do
				if child:IsA("BasePart") and child.CanCollide == true and child.Name ~= floatName then
					child.CanCollide = false
				end
			end
		end
	end
	Noclipping = game:GetService('RunService').Stepped:Connect(NoclipLoop)
	NoclipLoop()

 
_G.Vent:Play()
wait(.1)
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://5771441412", 1, 10)	
wait(1.5)
_G.Vent:AdjustSpeed(0)
wait(0.5)
	local location = mouse.Hit.p + Vector3.new(0,5,0)
	if (chr.HumanoidRootPart.Position - location).magnitude < 600 then
		tsteleportcooldown = true
		chr.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(location) + Vector3.new(0,2,0)
		if game.Lighting.TS.Value == false then
			spawn(function()
				wait(.1)
 
 
	_G.Unvent:Play()
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://5771441412", 1, 10)	
wait()
_G.Vent:Stop()
		if Noclipping then
		Noclipping:Disconnect()
	end
	Clip = true
			end)
		end
		wait(0)
		tsteleportcooldown = false
	end
end
end)
function vent()
    if activu == true then return end
	if tsteleportcooldown == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == false then return end
    	local speaker = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local args
local Noclipping = nil
    Clip = false
	wait(0.1)
	local function NoclipLoop()
		if Clip == false and speaker.Character ~= nil then
			for _, child in pairs(speaker.Character:GetDescendants()) do
				if child:IsA("BasePart") and child.CanCollide == true and child.Name ~= floatName then
					child.CanCollide = false
				end
			end
		end
	end
	Noclipping = game:GetService('RunService').Stepped:Connect(NoclipLoop)
	NoclipLoop()
   _G.Vent:Play()
   game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://5771441412", 1, 10)
   wait(1.5)
   _G.Vent:AdjustSpeed(0)
end
function unvent()
    if activu == true then return end
	if tsteleportcooldown == true then return end
	if fartmode == true then return end
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == false then return end
    		if Noclipping then
		Noclipping:Disconnect()
	end
    _G.Unvent:Play()
       game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://5771441412", 1, 10)
    wait(.5)
    _G.Vent:Stop()
    Clip = true
end
funny = false
mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(key)
    if key == "j" then
        if funny == false then
        funny = true
        vent()
    elseif funny == true then
        funny = false
        unvent()
    end
    end
    end)
local EHMMM = 0
local fartbarragecooldown = false
function fartbarrage()
	if activu == true then return end
	if fartbarragecooldown == true then return end
if mememode == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if fartmode == false then return end
	activu = true
	fartbarragecooldown = true
	bep = true
	de = mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(key)
	    if key == "e" then
	      bep = false
	    end
	end)
	humainbarrageanim:Play(0.1, 1, 0.75)
	human.WalkSpeed = 10
	human.JumpPower = 0
	repeat
	strongpunchevent:FireServer(Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1), Vector3.new(0.15, 0.075, 0.15), BrickColor.new("Brown"))
	strongpunchevent:FireServer(Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1), Vector3.new(0.125, 0.075, 0.125), BrickColor.new("Brown"))
		EHMMM = EHMMM + 1
		hito(rightarm, rightarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,15, 10, 0.1, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 0, "rbxassetid://", 0.5, Color3.new(1, 1, 0),"rbxassetid://4809574295", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 50)
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://4809574295", 1, 10)
		hito(leftarm, leftarm.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -1, 0) * CFrame.new(math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25), math.random(-0.25, 0.25)) ,15, 10, 0.1, 0.25, hrp.CFrame.lookVector * 0, "rbxassetid://", 0.5, Color3.new(1, 1, 0),"rbxassetid://4809574295", math.random(9, 11) / 10, math.random(9, 11) / 50)
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://4809574295", 1, 10)		
		wait(0.1)
	until bep == false or disabled.Value == true or EHMMM >= 30
	humainbarrageanim:Stop(0.1)
	human.WalkSpeed = 20
	human.JumpPower = 65
	activu = false
	EHMMM = 0
	wait(0)
	fartbarragecooldown = false
end

_G.healall = function()
    for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace.Entities:GetChildren()) do
        if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
            if (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < math.huge then
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SPOHRTZDMG:FireServer(v.Humanoid)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SPOHRTZDMG:FireServer(v.Humanoid)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SPOHRTZDMG:FireServer(v.Humanoid)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SPOHRTZDMG:FireServer(v.Humanoid)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SPOHRTZDMG:FireServer(v.Humanoid)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SPOHRTZDMG:FireServer(v.Humanoid)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SPOHRTZDMG:FireServer(v.Humanoid)
                	    	local limbuchoppa = "limbchop"
	    	local limbuchoppa2 = 
{
	    	[1] = v.Humanoid, 
	    	[2] = v.Torso.CFrame
}
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").MadeInHeavenHandler:FireServer(limbuchoppa,limbuchoppa2)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").MadeInHeavenHandler:FireServer(limbuchoppa,limbuchoppa2)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").MadeInHeavenHandler:FireServer(limbuchoppa,limbuchoppa2)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").MadeInHeavenHandler:FireServer(limbuchoppa,limbuchoppa2)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").MadeInHeavenHandler:FireServer(limbuchoppa,limbuchoppa2)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").MadeInHeavenHandler:FireServer(limbuchoppa,limbuchoppa2)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").MadeInHeavenHandler:FireServer(limbuchoppa,limbuchoppa2)

local movementcooldown = false
function movement()
	if activu == true then return end
	if amogusmode == true then return end
	if fnfmode == true then return end
if animemode == true then return end
	if attackmode == true then return end
	if movementcooldown == true then return end
	movementcooldown = true
	activu = true
	standjumpanim:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],0.25)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],0.5)
	--jumpsfx:Play()
	jumpevent:FireServer(BrickColor.new("Really red"))
	Bod = Instance.new("BodyPosition", hrp)
    Bod.maxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 100000, 100000)
    Bod.Position = hrp.CFrame*CFrame.new(0, 50, -75).p
	game.Debris:AddItem(Bod, 1)
	wait(1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Right Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Head"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Left Arm"],1)
	game.ReplicatedStorage.Transparency:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stand["Stand Torso"],1)
	activu = false
	wait()
	movementcooldown = false
end

function state()
chr:WaitForChild("Humanoid").StateChanged:Connect(function(OldState,NewState)
	NewStat = NewState
	OldStat = OldState
end)
end

if ntorso.Anchored == true then return end
if disabled.Value == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end
	punch()
end)

if ntorso.Anchored == true then return end
if disabled.Value == true then return end
if attackmode == false then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
	if balancedmode == true then return end
	humainpunch()
end)
mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
if ntorso.Anchored == true then return end
if disabled.Value == true then return end

	if key == "y" then
	if attackmode == false then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
		humainbarrage()
	end
	if key == "r" then
		strongpunch()
	end
	if key == "e" then
		barrage()
	end
	if key == "t" then
		yell()
	end
	if key == "y" then
		donut()
	end
	if key == "x" then
		block()
	end
	if key == "x" then
		fartblock()
	end
	if key == "e" then
	if fartmode == false then return end
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://4809574295", 1, 10)
		fartkick()
	end
	if key == "r" then
	if fartmode == false then return end
game.ReplicatedStorage.Damage:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame, 0, 0, Vector3.new(0,0,0), "", 0, Color3.new(0,0,0), "rbxassetid://5312369043", 1, 10)
		fartstrongpunch()
	end
	if key == "t" then
	if fartmode == false then return end
		fartbarrage()
	end
	if key == "f" then
	if attackmode == true then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
		ts()
	end
	if key == "z" then
		movement()
	end
	if key == "c" then
		dodge()
	end
		if key == "l" then
			if mouse.Target and mouse.Target.Parent then
				local Character = nil
				if mouse.Target.Parent:IsA("Model") and mouse.Target.Parent.Name == "Stand" then
					Character = mouse.Target.Parent.Parent
				elseif mouse.Target.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
					Character = mouse.Target.Parent
				end
				if Character then
					Perish(Character)
				end
			end
		end
		if key == "q" then
			if mouse.Target and mouse.Target.Parent then
				local Character = nil
				if mouse.Target.Parent:IsA("Model") and mouse.Target.Parent.Name == "Stand" then
					Character = mouse.Target.Parent.Parent
				elseif mouse.Target.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
					Character = mouse.Target.Parent
				end
				if Character then
					Perish2(Character)
				end
			end
		end
	if key == "g" then
		posefunc()
	end
	if key == "z" then
	if attackmode == false then return end
if fartmode == true then return end
		spin()
	end
	if key == "n" then
		taunt()
	end
end)


function hito(partoz, partcfr, magn, dmg, debtim, debtime, bodyfdire, effect, grow, color, sound, pitch, volume)
  for _, guy in pairs(workspace.Entities:GetChildren()) do
	if partoz.Anchored == true then return end
    if guy:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and guy:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and guy ~= chr and magn > (guy:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").Position - partoz.Position).magnitude and guy:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"):FindFirstChild("alabo") == nil then
      do
		if partoz.Anchored then return end
        local humz = guy:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        local horp = guy:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        damageevent:FireServer(humz, partcfr, dmg, debtime, bodyfdire, effect, grow, color, sound, pitch, volume)
	damageevent69:FireServer(humz, partcfr, dmg, debtime, bodyfdire, effect, grow, color, sound, pitch, volume)
		berserkevent:FireServer(humz)   
        local db = Instance.new("StringValue")
        db.Name = "alabo"
        db.Parent = horp
        delay(debtim, function()
          db:Destroy()
        end)
      end
    end

	if guy:FindFirstChild("Stand") and guy["Stand"]:FindFirstChild("Stand Torso") and guy ~= chr and guy ~= chr[stand.Name] and magn > (guy["Stand"]:FindFirstChild("Stand Torso").Position - partoz.Position).magnitude and guy:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"):FindFirstChild("alabo") == nil then

        local horp = guy:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        local humz = chr.Humanoid
        damageevent:FireServer(humz, partcfr, dmg, debtime, bodyfdire, effect, grow, color, sound, pitch, volume)

        end)
      end
    end
